UI/VideoOptionsInstructions=游戏进行或观看录像时，您可以按下CTRL-F11切换游戏内视频录制的开启与关闭。视频将以Theora OGV格式保存在您用户目录下的Starcraft II Videos文件夹中。录制高质量视频可能会极大地影响您的游戏体验。 /// You can toggle in-game video recording by pressing CTRL-F11 while playing a game or watching a replay. Videos are stored in your user directory's StarCraft II Videos folder in Theora OGV format. Recording high quality video may considerably slow down your game experience.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/AudioQuality=<c val="ffffff">音频质量：</c><n/>提高音频质量将获得更高的音频保真度，但会使文件体积增大。 /// <c val="ffffff">Audio Quality:</c><n/>Increasing audio quality will provide greater audio fidelity at a cost of larger video files.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/FrameRate=<c val="ffffff">帧率：</c><n/>帧率指每秒录制的帧的数量。帧率越高，所录制出的视频越流畅，但会使视频文件体积增大。录制高帧率的视频可能会影响游戏运行速度。 /// <c val="ffffff">Framerate:</c><n/>Framerate refers to the number of frames recorded per second. A higher framerate will result in smoother video playback at a cost of larger video files. Recording at a higher framerate may slow down your game experience.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/RecordAudioCheckbox=<c val="ffffff">开启音频录制：</c><n/>录制视频时包含声音。 /// <c val="ffffff">Enable Audio:</c><n/>Enables recording audio with your video.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/RecordTriggers=<c val="ffffff">触发器录制：</c><n/>开启该选项将允许游戏根据创建地图时预先设定的条件自动触发视频的录制。玩家创建地图时可以添加“开始录制视频”触发器，使视频的录制更为方便。如果您不想在某些地图中自动录制视频，请保持该选项的禁用状态。 /// <c val="ffffff">Record From Triggers:</c><n/>Enabling this option will allow you to record video from in-game triggers. Players can create maps with "MovieStartRecording" triggers to facilitate the creation of movies. Keep this option off if you do not want videos to automatically record on certain maps.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/Resolution=<c val="ffffff">分辨率：</c><n/>该选项决定了录制视频采用的像素数量。较高的分辨率对应较好的画面质量，但会延长录制时间。要获得最佳效果，请使用与您的屏幕高宽比相匹配的分辨率。 /// <c val="ffffff">Resolution:</c><n/>Determines the size in pixels of the recorded video. Higher resolutions have much better image quality, but they are slower to record. For best results, use a resolution that matches your game's aspect ratio.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/SlowGame=<c val="ffffff">录制视频时游戏减速：</c><n/>该选项决定了录制视频时是否减慢游戏速度以弥补性能下降造成的影响。开启此选项可以带来更好的视频效果，但在多人游戏中无法开启此选项。禁用此选项时录制的视频将受到帧数下降的影响，但音频部分不会受到影响。 /// <c val="ffffff">Slow Game while Recording:</c><n/>Determines whether or not game time will slow down to adjust for the performance drop while recording video. This will result in better looking videos, but it cannot be used while participating in multiplayer games. Videos recorded with this option disabled will record the drop in framerate, but your audio will be unaffected.
UI/VideoOptionsTooltips/VideoQuality=<c val="ffffff">视频质量：</c><n/>该选项决定了录制视频采用的压缩量。更高的视频质量会带来更好的画面质量，但会增加视频文件大小。 /// <c val="ffffff">Video Quality:</c><n/>Determines the amount of compression used when recording your video. Greater video quality will result in better image quality but much larger video files.
